CC2650 (both produced by Texas Instruments Company), ThunderBoard React, ThunderBoard Sense (both devices produced by Silicon Labs Company), Nordic Thingy:52 (produced by Nordic Semiconductor), WICED reading and notifying), use and display (in graphic and numeric ways) data from all sensors included in each of the SensorTags presented above;\r\n\r\n2. can trigger a visual or/and an audible warning
